\mbox{\Hypertarget{mmgcommon__private_8h_ae9022cab0e0d44ee3261e89f35a2be3d}\label{mmgcommon__private_8h_ae9022cab0e0d44ee3261e89f35a2be3d}}

\index{FUNCTION\_POINTER@{FUNCTION\_POINTER}!mmgcommon\_private.h@{mmgcommon\_private.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{FUNCTION\_POINTER}{FUNCTION\_POINTER}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \#define FUNCTION\+\_\+\+POINTER(\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{fproto }\end{DoxyParamCaption})~  \mbox{\hyperlink{mmgexterns_8c_a9bb322553103812c6e3b396a7235e310}{MMG\+\_\+\+EXTERN}} fproto \mbox{\hyperlink{mmgexterns_8c_af8ac8adc506ab4a471a7adc64c325bb8}{MMG\+\_\+\+ASSIGN\+\_\+\+NULL}}}


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em fproto} & function prototype\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
Expand automatically prototype of function pointer in .h/.c files depending on the definition of the MMG\+\_\+\+EXTERN and MMG\+\_\+\+ASSIGN\+\_\+\+NULL preprocessor variables\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item MMG\+\_\+\+EXTERN is setted to \char`\"{}extern\char`\"{} in the .h file and empty in the .c one;

\index{MMG5\_chkmaniball@{MMG5\_chkmaniball}!mmgcommon\_private.h@{mmgcommon\_private.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{MMG5\_chkmaniball()}{MMG5\_chkmaniball()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily int MMG5\+\_\+chkmaniball (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_a906478a19c4819942a0eea48823b774b}{MMG5\+\_\+p\+Mesh}}}]{mesh,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int}]{start,  }\item[{int8\+\_\+t}]{istart }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em mesh} & pointer toward the mesh structure. \\
\hline
{\em start} & index of starting tria. \\
\hline
{\em istart} & local index of point that we check (in tria {\itshape start}) \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
1 if the ball is manifold, 0 otherwise.
\end{DoxyReturn}
Check whether the ball of vertex i in tria start is manifold;

\begin{DoxyWarning}{Warning}
inxt\mbox{[}i\mbox{]} is an edge belonging to the implicit boundary. 
\end{DoxyWarning}
Step 1\+: Travel while another part of the implicit boundary is not met

Normal or multi-\/material mode\+: check for change in triangle references

Input reference preservation mode (mmgs --keep-\/ref option)\+: Check if we cross an isoref edge

Step 2\+: Check why the loop has ended

a./ Case where a boundary is hit\+: travel in the other sense from start, and make sure that a boundary is hit too

Ball is manifold if tested point is connected to two external edges

b./ General case\+: go on travelling until another implicit boundary is met

Ball is non-\/manifold if at least 3 boundary segments meeting at p

\end{DoxyReturn}
Check whether the resulting two subdomains occupying mesh are manifold. First check\+: check whether one triangle in the mesh has 3 boundary faces

Second check\+: check whether the configuration is manifold in the ball of each point; each vertex on the implicit boundary is caught in such a way that i1 inxt\mbox{[}i1\mbox{]} is one edge of the implicit boundary

Compute the mean metric at mesh points with a non-\/nul {\itshape s} field. At the beginning, for a given point {\itshape ip}, $ met->m[met->size * ip] $ contains the sum of n metrics and the {\itshape s} field of {\itshape ip} contains the number of metrics summed in the point. Set the flag of the processed points to 3.

\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em mesh} & pointer toward the mesh. \\
\hline
{\em met} & pointer toward the metric structure. \\
\hline
{\em pt} & pointer toward a triangle. \\
\hline
{\em np1} & global index of the first extremity of the edge. \\
\hline
{\em np2} & global index of the second extremity of the edge. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
-\/1 if no gradation is needed, else index of graded point.
\end{DoxyReturn}
Enforces gradation of metric in one extremity of edge \$f\mbox{[} np1; np2\mbox{]}\$f in tria {\itshape pt} with respect to the other, along the direction of the associated support curve first, then along the normal direction.

\begin{DoxyWarning}{Warning}
The gradation along the direction normal to the surface is made in an \char`\"{}isotropic way\char`\"{}.
\end{DoxyWarning}
\begin{DoxyRemark}{Remarks}
ALGIANE\+: a mettre  plat \+: dans le cas d\textquotesingle{}une mtrique trs aniso avec la grande taille quasiment dans la direction de l\textquotesingle{}arte on se retrouve  modifier la grande taille uniquement (car proche de l\textquotesingle{}arte) sauf que cette modification n\textquotesingle{}a quasi pas d\textquotesingle{}influence sur le calcul de la longueur d\textquotesingle{}arte. 
\end{DoxyRemark}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{MMG5\_ismaniball()}{MMG5\_ismaniball()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily int MMG5\+\_\+ismaniball (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_a906478a19c4819942a0eea48823b774b}{MMG5\+\_\+p\+Mesh}}}]{mesh,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_a73ac506fe087cc604bb892e46373719a}{MMG5\+\_\+p\+Sol}}}]{sol,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int}]{start,  }\item[{int8\+\_\+t}]{istart }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em mesh} & pointer toward the mesh structure. \\
\hline
{\em sol} & pointer toward the level-\/set values. \\
\hline
{\em start} & index of the starting tria \\
\hline
{\em istart} & local index (inside the tria {\itshape start}) of the vertex that we check. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
1 if success, 0 if fail
\end{DoxyReturn}
Check whether snapping the value of vertex {\itshape istart} of {\itshape start} to 0 exactly leads to a non manifold situation.

\begin{DoxyWarning}{Warning}
\+: we assume that the triangle {\itshape start} has vertex {\itshape istart} with value 0 and the other two with changing values. 
\end{DoxyWarning}

\begin{DoxyRemark}{Remarks}
the ph-\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}s field computation is useless in mmgs.

\+: as all triangles are mesh boundaries, we do not need to mark their adges as MG\+\_\+\+BDY so the MG\+\_\+\+BDY tag may be used inside geometrical triangles (external non-\/parallel, or internal parallel) to tag edges on the intersection with purely parallel (non-\/geometrical) triangles. The MG\+\_\+\+PARBDYBDY tag is also added, as it does not have a supporting triangle to inherit this tag from. 
\end{DoxyRemark}

\index{MMG5\_MultiMat\_init@{MMG5\_MultiMat\_init}!mmgcommon\_private.h@{mmgcommon\_private.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{MMG5\_MultiMat\_init()}{MMG5\_MultiMat\_init()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily int MMG5\+\_\+\+Multi\+Mat\+\_\+init (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_a906478a19c4819942a0eea48823b774b}{MMG5\+\_\+p\+Mesh}}}]{mesh }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em mesh} & pointer toward the mesh structure. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
1 if success, 0 if fail.
\end{DoxyReturn}
Initialize handling of multimaterial mode.

An indexed table of materials has been provided by the \mbox{\hyperlink{structMMG5__Mat}{MMG5\+\_\+\+Mat}} datatype in the form\+:\hypertarget{mmgcommon__private_8h_autotoc_md30}{}\doxysubsubsection{index $\vert$ dospl       $\vert$ ref       $\vert$ rin       $\vert$ rex}\label{mmgcommon__private_8h_autotoc_md30}
0 $\vert$ dospl\+\_\+0 $\vert$ ref\+\_\+0 $\vert$ rin\+\_\+0 $\vert$ rex\+\_\+0 ... $\vert$ ... $\vert$ ... $\vert$ ... $\vert$ k $\vert$ dospl\+\_\+k $\vert$ ref\+\_\+k $\vert$ rin\+\_\+k $\vert$ rex\+\_\+k ... $\vert$ ... $\vert$ ... $\vert$ ... $\vert$ n-\/1 $\vert$ dospl\+\_\+\{n-\/1\} $\vert$ ref\+\_\+\{n-\/1\} $\vert$ rin\+\_\+\{n-\/1\} $\vert$ rex\+\_\+\{n-\/1\}

where dospl is the split/preserve attribute of the material, and rin,rex are its child materials (if dospl). Viceversa, ref is the parent material for rin,rex.

Here a lookup table for material references is built through trivial hashing for all references (both parent and child materials) with the key\+:

key = ref -\/ ref\+\_\+min, ref\+\_\+min = min\+\_\+\{k = 0,n-\/1\} (ref\+\_\+k, rin\+\_\+k, rex\+\_\+k)

For all references, it is important to store
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item the index k of the row in the original table,
\item the characteristic attribute (parent-\/split, parent-\/preserve, child-\/interior, child-\/exterior) of the material.
\end{DoxyItemize}

Since dospl = 0 or 1, MG\+\_\+\+PLUS = 2, and MG\+\_\+\+MINUS = 3

we can store the attribute as dospl (for the parent material) or MG\+\_\+\+MINUS/ MG\+\_\+\+PLUS (for the child materials), with its value ranging between 0 and 3.

A convenient entry to store both the index and the attribute in the lookup table is thus\+:

entry = 4$\ast$(index+1) + attribute

leading to a lookup table in the form (the key ordering is only an example)\+:\hypertarget{mmgcommon__private_8h_autotoc_md31}{}\doxysubsubsection{key   $\vert$ entry}\label{mmgcommon__private_8h_autotoc_md31}
... $\vert$ ... ref\+\_\+k $\vert$ 4$\ast$(k+1)+dospl\+\_\+k ... $\vert$ ... rin\+\_\+k $\vert$ 4$\ast$(k+1)+MG\+\_\+\+MINUS ... $\vert$ ... rex\+\_\+k $\vert$ 4$\ast$(k+1)+MG\+\_\+\+PLUS ... $\vert$ ...

where the index and the attribute of the material can be retrieved as

index = entry / 4 -\/1 attribute = entry \% 4

What if two materials have the same reference?
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item child references should be distinct (the entry in the lookup table would be overwritten),
\item a parent material can have itself as child (a positive attribute would say it should be split, the attribute value would say if it is interior or exterior). Thus, each of the maps parent-\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}child\+\_\+in and parent-\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}child\+\_\+ext is injective, but a fixed point is allowed.
\end{DoxyItemize}

Why child materials should be different?
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item because on failure it is necessary to recover the parent references and apply them on the tetrahedra to restore the starting materials distribution. 
\end{DoxyItemize}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily double MMG5\+\_\+rid\+Size\+In\+Normal\+Dir (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_a906478a19c4819942a0eea48823b774b}{MMG5\+\_\+p\+Mesh}}}]{,  }\item[{int}]{,  }\item[{double $\ast$}]{,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{mmgcommon__private_8h_a76da89d731fcac55dc78dcd0e297da1e}{MMG5\+\_\+p\+Bezier}}}]{,  }\item[{double}]{,  }\item[{double}]{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

\mbox{\Hypertarget{mmgcommon__private_8h_ac7168aea99826279ee2158a54bd5128c}\label{mmgcommon__private_8h_ac7168aea99826279ee2158a54bd5128c}} 
\index{mmgcommon\_private.h@{mmgcommon\_private.h}!MMG5\_ridSizeInTangentDir@{MMG5\_ridSizeInTangentDir}}
\index{MMG5\_ridSizeInTangentDir@{MMG5\_ridSizeInTangentDir}!mmgcommon\_private.h@{mmgcommon\_private.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{MMG5\_ridSizeInTangentDir()}{MMG5\_ridSizeInTangentDir()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily double MMG5\+\_\+rid\+Size\+In\+Tangent\+Dir (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_a906478a19c4819942a0eea48823b774b}{MMG5\+\_\+p\+Mesh}}}]{mesh,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_a8a626fbb189129e6f22bde1246f7bb25}{MMG5\+\_\+p\+Point}}}]{p0,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int}]{idp,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int $\ast$}]{iprid,  }\item[{double}]{isqhmin,  }\item[{double}]{isqhmax }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em mesh} & pointer toward the mesh structure. \\
\hline
{\em p0} & pointer toward the point at which we define the metric. \\
\hline
{\em idp} & global index of the point at which we define the metric. \\
\hline
{\em iprid} & pointer toward the two extremities of the ridge. \\
\hline
{\em isqhmin} & minimum edge size. \\
\hline
{\em isqhmax} & maximum edge size. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
the computed ridge size in the tangent direction.
\end{DoxyReturn}
Compute the specific size that we want to apply to a ridge in the direction of the tangent of the ridge. This wanted size is computed as using the majoration of the haudorff distance between a triangle and its ideal curve approximation by the Hessian of the signed distance function to the ideal surface.

\[
d^H(\partial \Omega,S_T) \leq \displaystyle\frac{1}{2}\left(
\frac{d-1}{d} \right)^2 \max\limits_{T\in S_T} \max\limits_{x \in T
} \max\limits_{y,z \in T} \langle \left| H(d_\omega)(x) \right|
yz,yz\rangle.
\]

where $ d^H(\partial \Omega,S_T) $ is the distance between the triangle $S_T$ and the ideal boundary (reconstructed using cubic Bezier patches) $ \partial \Omega $, $ d$ is the mesh dimension and $
  H(d_\Omega) $ is the hessian matrix of the signed distance function to $
  \Omega $.

For all $ x \in \partial \Omega $, $H(d_\omega)(x)$ is the second fundamental form whose eigenvalues are the principal curvatures ( $\kappa_1
  $ and $ \kappa_2 $) of $ \partial \Omega $ at $ x $ so the previous formula can be rewritten as\+:  \[
d^H(\partial \Omega,S_T) \leq \displaystyle\frac{1}{2}\left(
\frac{d-1}{d} \right)^2 \max( \left|\kappa_1\right|,\left|\kappa_2\right|).
\]

As we want to respect the imposed the {\itshape hausd} threshold and we are interessed to get the wanted size along the tangent direction at the ridge point only, finally, m is computed as

\[
m = \kappa \frac{1}{2\textrm{hausd}}
\left(\frac{d-1}{d} \right)^2.
\]

See Theorem 1 of \cite{dapogny2014three}. 

Definition at line \mbox{\hyperlink{anisosiz_8c_source_l00764}{764}} of file \mbox{\hyperlink{anisosiz_8c_source}{anisosiz.\+c}}.
